I looked up the $75 fee and SHOULD NOT have been charged it, since I am the owner/occupier of the house. I Called and they just told me "oh we don't tell you about exemptions you should have a lawyer" I told her I absolutely DID have a lawyer do that for me, and she stated it was their responsibility. Ridiculous that the employee could have just asked me if I was occupying the home, and told me to fill out another sheet of paper and couldn't or wouldn't be bothered. Since when it is a lawyers responsibility, as they are the one charging the fees for the service?  I did look at the website before hand and did not see that anywhere. A shame, the world be a much better place if we could all just be a little kinder and help one another.</review>

< Review>
Hard to really rate a smog check service. Every time I take my car in, they give it a passing report. Is that good? Or is that bad? I'll assume that the car is actually not polluting more than current standards allow and call it "good".
They successfully upload the pass result to the DMV systems so that I can complete the registration the next day, so that's good.
The "waiting area" is kinda iffy. Thankfully they've never made me wait there for too long.
The guy handling intakes was polite and efficient.
All in all, a good enough smog check service, I think.< /Review>

<user_id>117369842481516893220< /user_id><name>Veronica Santana< /name>< Date>

< rating>
4< /rating>
< Text>
The sushi rolls are awesome!!
The appetizers are good but need some work
The teriyaki chicken is delicious!
The restaurant is kind of small and has limited seating
Not many options to drink, no alcohol/sake/etc.
The restroom is in the back and theres only 1 for both women and men, must lock it when in use and after finish using
The wait times for your food are normal, not fast or slow and they let you know how long the wait will be if you order a baked dish
The staff is always polite and never seem grumpy even though...
They get very busy at times since the food is so good for the price

The only real cons are more about the setting and not the food. Limited Seating, Busy Parking lot (carwash on same lot) and Small restaurant with separate bathroom.

I use to go from sushi spot to sushi spot trying each out and being disappointed in the taste vs the price but here the sushi is great for the price. I now come here at least once a week.<//Text>
